Recently, he seems to have relapsed in his bowel, although he has had positive biopsies in the past. He is entirely asymptomatic. His iron levels are normal and he has no diarrhea. He denies any abdominal pain and his weight is stable. Full body CT scan and PET scan revealed no PET CT evidence of malignancy. There are small abdominal lymph nodes, but they are not PET avid. Thus, he appears to have involvement only of his bowel at this point. I do feel a supraclavicular lymph node, which may be secondary to the lymphoma as well.   The patient was discussed at lymphoma conference. The question is whether he needs any treatment at all and what he should be treated with. He does have quite diffuse involvement of his bowel and my feeling would be that treatment is indicated. Other people in conference felt that observation only would be a reasonable approach. Treatment could be with just single agent Rituxan, which I think would be reasonable for him. Unfortunately, there really is not anything to follow. He also has done well with single agent <DRUG>fludarabine</DRUG></REASON> , which would be another option.   PL
